## Instruction

My personal information is all stored in memory. Based on the course information on Canvas, as well as my assignment and quiz submission status. Find all my unfinished course assignments and quizzes that have to be completed, organize the information according to the required fields in the workspace's CSV header, keeping the format consistent with these examples, and complete these CSV files. In filling the files, please fill the quizzes/assignments in chronological order by their deadlines (DDL), and for quizzes/assignmen with the same DDL, sort them in the dictionary order of the class code. You should directly edit in the given 2 CSV files without changing their file names.

```python 
import os
import pandas as pd

# Check workspace directory
workspace_dir = "/workspace/dumps/workspace"
print("Files in workspace:")
for file in os.listdir(workspace_dir):
    print(f"  {file}")

# Read the CSV files to see their headers and format
csv_files = [f for f in os.listdir(workspace_dir) if f.endswith('.csv')]
print(f"\nFound CSV files: {csv_files}")

for csv_file in csv_files:
    file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, csv_file)
    print(f"\n=== {csv_file} ===")
    try:
        df = pd.read_csv(file_path)
        print("Headers:", list(df.columns))
        print("Shape:", df.shape)
        if not df.empty:
            print("First few rows:")
            print(df.head())
        else:
            print("File is empty")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error reading {csv_file}: {e}")
```
</div>

```python 
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
import os

# Sort assignments by deadline, then by course code
unfinished_assignments_sorted = sorted(unfinished_assignments, key=lambda x: (x['deadline'], x['course_code']))
unfinished_quizzes_sorted = sorted(unfinished_quizzes, key=lambda x: (x['deadline'], x['course_code']))

print("Assignments sorted by deadline:")
for assignment in unfinished_assignments_sorted:
    print(f"  {assignment['deadline']} - {assignment['course_code']}: {assignment['assignment_title']}")

print("\nQuizzes sorted by deadline:")
for quiz in unfinished_quizzes_sorted:
    print(f"  {quiz['deadline']} - {quiz['course_code']}: {quiz['quiz_title']}")

# Prepare assignment data for CSV
assignment_data = []
for assignment in unfinished_assignments_sorted:
    assignment_data.append({
        'course_code': assignment['course_code'],
        'course_name': assignment['course_name'],
        'assignment_title': assignment['assignment_title'],
        'description': assignment['description'],
        'deadline': assignment['deadline'],
        'points_possible': assignment['points_possible']
    })

# Prepare quiz data for CSV
quiz_data = []
for quiz in unfinished_quizzes_sorted:
    quiz_data.append({
        'course_code': quiz['course_code'],
        'course_name': quiz['course_name'],
        'credits': quiz['credits'],
        'quiz_title': quiz['quiz_title'],
        'number_of_questions': quiz['number_of_questions'],
        'time_limit': quiz['time_limit'],
        'allowed_attempts': quiz['allowed_attempts'],
        'scoring_policy': quiz['scoring_policy'],
        'points_possible': quiz['points_possible'],
        'deadline': quiz['deadline']
    })

print(f"\nPrepared {len(assignment_data)} assignments and {len(quiz_data)} quizzes for CSV files")
```

```python 
import pandas as pd
import os

workspace_dir = "/workspace/dumps/workspace"

# Prepare assignment data for CSV
assignment_data = []
for assignment in unfinished_assignments_sorted:
    assignment_data.append({
        'course_code': assignment['course_code'],
        'course_name': assignment['course_name'],
        'assignment_title': assignment['assignment_title'],
        'description': assignment['description'],
        'deadline': assignment['deadline'],
        'points_possible': assignment['points_possible']
    })

# Prepare quiz data for CSV
quiz_data = []
for quiz in unfinished_quizzes_sorted:
    quiz_data.append({
        'course_code': quiz['course_code'],
        'course_name': quiz['course_name'],
        'credits': quiz['credits'],
        'quiz_title': quiz['quiz_title'],
        'number_of_questions': quiz['number_of_questions'],
        'time_limit': quiz['time_limit'],
        'allowed_attempts': quiz['allowed_attempts'],
        'scoring_policy': quiz['scoring_policy'],
        'points_possible': quiz['points_possible'],
        'deadline': quiz['deadline']
    })

# Create DataFrames
assignments_df = pd.DataFrame(assignment_data)
quizzes_df = pd.DataFrame(quiz_data)

# Write to CSV files
assignments_csv_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, "assignment_info.csv")
quizzes_csv_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, "quiz_info.csv")

assignments_df.to_csv(assignments_csv_path, index=False)
quizzes_df.to_csv(quizzes_csv_path, index=False)

print(f"Successfully updated assignment_info.csv with {len(assignment_data)} assignments")
print(f"Successfully updated quiz_info.csv with {len(quiz_data)} quizzes")

# Display the first few rows to verify
print("\nAssignment CSV content:")
print(assignments_df.head())

print("\nQuiz CSV content:")
print(quizzes_df.head())
```

```python 
import pandas as pd
import os

workspace_dir = "/workspace/dumps/workspace"

# Read and display the final CSV files
assignments_df = pd.read_csv(os.path.join(workspace_dir, "assignment_info.csv"))
quizzes_df = pd.read_csv(os.path.join(workspace_dir, "quiz_info.csv"))

print("=== ASSIGNMENT_INFO.CSV ===")
print("Headers:", list(assignments_df.columns))
print("Shape:", assignments_df.shape)
print("\nContent:")
for i, row in assignments_df.iterrows():
    print(f"{i+1}. {row['course_code']} - {row['assignment_title']} (Due: {row['deadline']}, Points: {row['points_possible']})")

print("\n=== QUIZ_INFO.CSV ===")
print("Headers:", list(quizzes_df.columns))
print("Shape:", quizzes_df.shape)
print("\nContent:")
for i, row in quizzes_df.iterrows():
    print(f"{i+1}. {row['course_code']} - {row['quiz_title']} (Due: {row['deadline']}, Points: {row['points_possible']})")

print("\n=== SUMMARY ===")
print(f"Total unfinished assignments: {len(assignments_df)}")
print(f"Total unfinished quizzes: {len(quizzes_df)}")
print("All items are sorted by deadline, then by course code in dictionary order.")
print("CSV files have been successfully updated with your unfinished coursework.")
```

```python 
]

def sort_key(item):
    return (item["due_at"], item["course_code"])

unfinished_quizzes.sort(key=sort_key)
unfinished_assignments.sort(key=sort_key)

with open("/workspace/dumps/workspace/unfinished_quizzes.csv", "w", newline="") as f:
    writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=["course_code", "course_name", "name", "due_at", "points_possible"])
    writer.writeheader()
    writer.writerows(unfinished_quizzes)

with open("/workspace/dumps/workspace/unfinished_assignments.csv", "w", newline="") as f:
    writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=["course_code", "course_name", "name", "due_at", "points_possible"])
    writer.writeheader()
    writer.writerows(unfinished_assignments)

print("Successfully updated unfinished_assignments.csv and unfinished_quizzes.csv")
```
